----------------------------------------
// the interesting parts:

{
  key: "goTo",
  value: function(e) {
      var t = document.createElement("a");
      t.href = e, t.hostname !== window.location.hostname ? window.open(e, "_blank", "noopener") : window.location = t.href
  }
}

----------------------------------------
// workaround (not elegant):

<script>
  document.createElement = function(){return null}
</script

----------------------------------------
// workaround (more general-purpose):

<script>
  unsafeWindow.document.close()      // close the current document
  unsafeWindow.document.open()       // open a new document, which removes all DOM from previous document and cancels all running scripts
  unsafeWindow.document.write(html)  // add DOM elements to new document
  unsafeWindow.document.close()
</script

notes:
======
* this approach assumes that there is nothing of any value in the previous document's DOM,
  which is the case on pages for a show,
  but not true for pages with a video

* annecdotally, only pages for a show experience this continuous reload issue

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
